<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="List_by_country">List by country</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: List by country">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Albania">Albania</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Albania">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Albania" title="Albania">Albania</a>, Children's Day (Festa e femijeve) is celebrated on 1 June.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Argentina">Argentina</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Argentina">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a>, Children's Day (Día del Niño) is celebrated on the third Sunday of August.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Armenia">Armenia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Armenia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Armenia" title="Armenia">Armenia</a>, Children's Day is celebrated on 1 June.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Australia">Australia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Australia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Children's Week is an annual event celebrated in Australia during the fourth week in October, from the Saturday before Universal Children's Day to the following Sunday. It was established as a holiday in 1954. Until 1977 Child Care Week was held in various Australian states and territories focusing on children in care or those in institutions. It was held at different times. In 1984 it was decided to coordinate a national week to include all children.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Azerbaijan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Azerbaijan" title="Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a>, Children's Day is celebrated on 1 June.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Bangladesh">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Since 2009 <a href="/wiki/JAAGO_Foundation" title="JAAGO Foundation">JAAGO Foundation</a> has been celebrating International Children's Day (বিশ্ব শিশু দিবস) throughout Bangladesh by engaging youth and creating awareness about children's right on 20 November which is the declared Universal Children's Day by <a href="/wiki/United_Nation" class="mw-redirect" title="United Nation">United Nation</a>. After this movement gained a lot of attraction, <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a> started celebrating, Children's Day on 17 March on the birthday of the Father of the Nation Bangabandhu <a href="/wiki/Sheikh_Mujibur_Rahman" title="Sheikh Mujibur Rahman">Sheikh Mujibur Rahman</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bolivia">Bolivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Bolivia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Children's day in Bolivia was first established in 1954. Google made a Google Doodle celebrating this holiday on 13 April 2019. Although the holiday is celebrated on 12 April not the 13th.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bosnia_and_Herzegovina">Bosnia and Herzegovina</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Bosnia and Herzegovina">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Bosnia_and_Herzegovina" title="Bosnia and Herzegovina">Bosnia and Herzegovina</a>, Children's Day was established as a holiday in 1993.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Brazil">Brazil</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Brazil">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>, Children's Day (In <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_language" title="Portuguese language">Portuguese</a>: Dia das Crianças) is celebrated on 12 October, coinciding with <a href="/wiki/Our_Lady_of_Aparecida" title="Our Lady of Aparecida">Our Lady of Aparecida</a>'s day, the country's <a href="/wiki/Patron_Saint" class="mw-redirect" title="Patron Saint">Patron Saint</a> holiday. It is also the day of the discovery of America (Columbus Day), in reference to the "New Continent". In Brazil Children's day is celebrated by kids receiving presents from their parents.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bulgaria">Bulgaria</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Bulgaria">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Bulgaria" title="Bulgaria">Bulgaria</a>, Children's day (Ден на детето) is celebrated on 1 June.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Traditionally kids receive very special attention from their family, including Birthday-like presents. In the past, all drivers were expected to drive with their lights on all day long to demonstrate extra vigilance over children's safety. Now it is compulsory to drive with the lights on every day of the year.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cambodia">Cambodia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Cambodia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Cambodia" title="Cambodia">Cambodia</a>. Children's Day is celebrated on 1 June.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cameroon">Cameroon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Cameroon">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Cameroon" title="Cameroon">Cameroon</a>, Children's Day was established as a holiday in 1990.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Canada">Canada</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Canada">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>National Child Day has been proclaimed across <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a> since 1993 to commemorate the United Nations' adoption of two documents centered on children's rights: the United Nations Declaration of the Rights of the Child on 20 November 1959, and the United Nations Convention on the Rights of the Child on 20 November 1989.<sup id="cite_ref-Plan_Canada_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Plan_Canada-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> The "Child Day Act" outlines human rights to which children, under the age of 18, are entitled by law. This Act promotes awareness and teaches children that they have rights, like adults do, under the law.<sup id="cite_ref-Plan_Canada_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Plan_Canada-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> The date of celebration is 20 November.<sup id="cite_ref-Plan_Canada_25-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Plan_Canada-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Central_Africa">Central Africa</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Central Africa">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Republic of the Congo">Congo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Democratic Republic of the Congo">Congo DR</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cameroon" title="Cameroon">Cameroon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Equatorial_Guinea" title="Equatorial Guinea">Equatorial Guinea</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gabon" title="Gabon">Gabon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chad" title="Chad">Chad</a>, <a href="/wiki/Central_African_Republic" title="Central African Republic">Central African Republic</a>, Children's Day is celebrated on 25 December to honor all the children there.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Chile">Chile</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Chile">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chile</a>, Children's Day is officially recognized and assigned to the first Wednesday of October. However, it is observed on the second Sunday of August.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> It retains none of the international flavors as a day to recognize the needs of or rights of children, but is observed merely as a commercial holiday dedicated to buying toys for children.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="China">China</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: China">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="infobox" style="width:22em"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold;background-color:#b0c4de">Children's Day (PRC)</th></tr><tr style="display:none;"><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center"></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="font-weight:normal;"><a href="/wiki/Simplified_Chinese_characters" title="Simplified Chinese characters">Simplified Chinese</a></th><td><span lang="zh-Hans" style="font-size:1rem;" title="Chinese language text">六一国际儿童节</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="font-weight:normal;"><a href="/wiki/Traditional_Chinese_characters" title="Traditional Chinese characters">Traditional&#160;Chinese</a></th><td><span lang="zh-Hant" style="font-size:1rem;" title="Chinese language text">六一國際兒童節</span></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><table class="collapsible collapsed" style="padding:0;border:none;margin:-3px;width:auto;min-width:100%;font-size:100%;clear:none;float:none;background-color:transparent"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold;font-size: 100%; text-align: left; background-color: #f9ffbc;">Transcriptions</th></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;background-color: #dcffc9;"><a href="/wiki/Standard_Chinese" title="Standard Chinese">Standard Mandarin</a></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="font-weight:normal;"><a href="/wiki/Hanyu_Pinyin" class="mw-redirect" title="Hanyu Pinyin">Hanyu Pinyin</a></th><td><span style="font-style:normal" lang="zh-Latn" title="Chinese-language romanization">Liù Yī Guójì Értóng Jié</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="font-weight:normal;"><a href="/wiki/Wade%E2%80%93Giles" title="Wade–Giles">Wade–Giles</a></th><td><span style="font-style:normal" lang="zh-Latn" title="Chinese-language romanization">Liu<sup>4</sup>-i<sup>1</sup> Kuo<sup>2</sup>-chi<sup>4</sup> Erh<sup>2</sup>-t'ung<sup>2</sup> Chieh<sup>2</sup></span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="font-weight:normal;"><a href="/wiki/Yale_romanization_of_Mandarin" title="Yale romanization of Mandarin">Yale Romanization</a></th><td><span style="font-style:normal" lang="zh-Latn" title="Chinese-language romanization">lyou4 yi1 gwo2 ji4 er2 tung2 jye2</span></td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;background-color: #dcffc9;"><a href="/wiki/Cantonese" title="Cantonese">Yue: Cantonese</a></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="font-weight:normal;"><a href="/wiki/Jyutping" title="Jyutping">Jyutping</a></th><td><span style="font-style:normal" lang="yue-Latn" title="Yue Chinese-language romanization">luk6 jat1 gwok3 zai3 ji4 tung4 zit3</span></td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr style="display:none"><td colspan="2">
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>In the <b><a href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" class="mw-redirect" title="People&#39;s Republic of China">People's Republic of China</a></b>, Children's Day is celebrated on 1 June and is formally known as "the June 1 International Children's Day" . When the People's Republic of China was first established in 1949, the State Council (Cabinet) designated a half-day holiday for all primary schools on 1 June. This was later made into a full day's break in 1956 with <i>The Announcement by the State Council to make 1 June Children's Day a One-Day Holiday</i>. Schools usually hold activities such as children's performances, camping trips, or free movies on Children's Day or the day before to allow students to have fun. Children of civil servants might also receive small gifts from the government until they are fourteen, and Civil servants who have children sometimes have a half-day holiday on 1 June to spend more time with their children. Entrance and set out ceremonies of the <a href="/wiki/Young_Pioneers_of_China" title="Young Pioneers of China">Young Pioneers of China</a> are usually held on 1 June as well. The entrance of children under 14 into the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_City" title="Forbidden City">Forbidden City</a> is free on 1 June, while each accompanying adult gets 50% off.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Colombia">Colombia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Colombia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">Colombia</a>, Children's Day is celebrated on the last Saturday of April. It was established as a holiday in 2001.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Costa_Rica">Costa Rica</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Costa Rica">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Costa_Rica" title="Costa Rica">Costa Rica</a>, Children's Day is celebrated on 9 September.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Croatia">Croatia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Croatia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Croatia" title="Croatia">Croatia</a>, Children's Day is celebrated on 11 November.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cuba">Cuba</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Cuba">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a>, Children's Day is celebrated on the third Sunday of July.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Czech_Republic">Czech Republic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Czech Republic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic" title="Czech Republic">Czech Republic</a>, Children's Day (<i>Mezinárodní den dětí</i>) is celebrated on 1 June.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ecuador">Ecuador</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Ecuador">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Ecuador" title="Ecuador">Ecuador</a>, Children's Day (Día del Niño) is celebrated on 1 June. Generally, kids up to 12 years old receive presents.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Festival_infantil.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Festival_infantil.JPG/220px-Festival_infantil.JPG" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Festival_infantil.JPG/330px-Festival_infantil.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Festival_infantil.JPG/440px-Festival_infantil.JPG 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="480" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Festival_infantil.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Children's day (Día del Niño) in <a href="/wiki/Ecuador" title="Ecuador">Ecuador</a></div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Egypt">Egypt</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Egypt">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a>, Children's Day is celebrated every 20 November with festivals and games for children.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Eritrea">Eritrea</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Eritrea">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Eritrea" title="Eritrea">Eritrea</a>, Children's Day is celebrated on 8 December.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Finland">Finland</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Finland">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Finland" title="Finland">Finland</a>, Children's Day is known as Day of Children's Rights and is celebrated on 20 November.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Former_and_current_communist_and_socialist_countries">Former and current communist and socialist countries</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Former and current communist and socialist countries">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:1997._Stamp_of_Belarus_0246.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b9/1997._Stamp_of_Belarus_0246.jpg/220px-1997._Stamp_of_Belarus_0246.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="158" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b9/1997._Stamp_of_Belarus_0246.jpg/330px-1997._Stamp_of_Belarus_0246.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b9/1997._Stamp_of_Belarus_0246.jpg 2x" data-file-width="349" data-file-height="250" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:1997._Stamp_of_Belarus_0246.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>1997 stamp of <a href="/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus">Belarus</a></div></div></div>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>, as well as other former <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet Union</a> states, including <a href="/wiki/Armenia" title="Armenia">Armenia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Azerbaijan" title="Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus">Belarus</a>, <a href="/wiki/Estonia" title="Estonia">Estonia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kazakhstan" title="Kazakhstan">Kazakhstan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kyrgyzstan" title="Kyrgyzstan">Kyrgyzstan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Latvia" title="Latvia">Latvia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lithuania" title="Lithuania">Lithuania</a>, <a href="/wiki/Moldova" title="Moldova">Moldova</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tajikistan" title="Tajikistan">Tajikistan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Turkmenistan" title="Turkmenistan">Turkmenistan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a>, <a href="/wiki/Uzbekistan" title="Uzbekistan">Uzbekistan</a>, other former or current <a href="/wiki/Communism" title="Communism">communist</a> states, <a href="/wiki/Albania" title="Albania">Albania</a>, <a href="/wiki/Angola" title="Angola">Angola</a>, <a href="/wiki/Benin" title="Benin">Benin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bosnia_and_Herzegovina" title="Bosnia and Herzegovina">Bosnia and Herzegovina</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bulgaria" title="Bulgaria">Bulgaria</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cambodia" title="Cambodia">Cambodia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Croatia" title="Croatia">Croatia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a>, <a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic" title="Czech Republic">Czech Republic</a>, <a href="/wiki/Slovakia" title="Slovakia">Slovakia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ethiopia" title="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</a>, <a href="/wiki/German_Democratic_Republic" class="mw-redirect" title="German Democratic Republic">East Germany</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kosovo" title="Kosovo">Kosovo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Laos" title="Laos">Laos</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mongolia" title="Mongolia">Mongolia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Montenegro" title="Montenegro">Montenegro</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mozambique" title="Mozambique">Mozambique</a>, <a href="/wiki/North_Macedonia" title="North Macedonia">North Macedonia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Romania" title="Romania">Romania</a>, <a href="/wiki/Serbia" title="Serbia">Serbia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Slovenia" title="Slovenia">Slovenia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tanzania" title="Tanzania">Tanzania</a> and <a href="/wiki/South_Yemen" title="South Yemen">Yemen</a>, and to the lesser extent, <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a> (due to the migration of its Soviet Jewish population) Children's Day is celebrated on 1 June.
</p><p>This list includes 25 countries which regained independence from <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">USSR</a>, seceded from <a href="/wiki/Socialist_Federal_Republic_of_Yugoslavia" title="Socialist Federal Republic of Yugoslavia">Yugoslavia Federation</a>, as well as <a href="/wiki/Czechoslovakia" title="Czechoslovakia">Czechoslovakia</a> and <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Democratic_Republic_of_Ethiopia" title="People&#39;s Democratic Republic of Ethiopia">Ethiopia</a> after their respective splits. 
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>, a pro-Soviet aligned state<sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Dates_and_numbers#Chronological_items" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers"><span title="The time period mentioned near this tag is ambiguous. (October 2019)">when?</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>, officially celebrates Children's Day of 14 November.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Germany">Germany</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Germany">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a>, during the <a href="/wiki/Cold_War" title="Cold War">Cold War</a>, Children's Day (Kindertag) was handled quite differently in <a href="/wiki/West_Germany" title="West Germany">West Germany</a> and <a href="/wiki/East_Germany" title="East Germany">East Germany</a>. While East Germany (GDR) celebrated <i>International Children's Day</i> (<i lang="de" title="German language text">Internationaler Kindertag</i>) on 1 June, <a href="/wiki/West_Germany" title="West Germany">West Germany</a> (FRG) celebrated <i>Universal Children's Day</i> (<i lang="de" title="German language text">Weltkindertag</i>) on 20 September.
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Convention_(norm)" title="Convention (norm)">customs</a> of Children's Day was also significantly different in West and East Germany. In East Germany, the holiday was introduced in 1950 and was from then held on a yearly basis for the children. On this day of the year, children would typically be congratulated and would receive presents from their parents and did special activities in <a href="/wiki/School" title="School">school</a>, such as field trips and the like.
</p><p>In West Germany, Children's Day <i>Universal Children's Day</i> laid its emphasis not on games and presents, but more on political efforts to strengthen <a href="/wiki/Children%27s_rights" title="Children&#39;s rights">children's rights</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (April 2014)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> (See <a href="/wiki/Jugendamt" title="Jugendamt">Jugendamt</a>.)
</p><p>After the <a href="/wiki/German_reunification" title="German reunification">reunification of East and West Germany</a> occurred in 1990, <i>Universal Children's Day</i> has become official for whole Germany. This, however, was not accepted by large parts of the East German population. Most parents still celebrate Children's Day on the former date of 1 June, and public events pertaining to Children's Day take place on 20 September (<i>Weltkindertag</i>).<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Greece">Greece</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Greece">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greece</a>, Children's Day was established in 1989.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Guatemala">Guatemala</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Guatemala">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Guatemala" title="Guatemala">Guatemala</a>, Children's Day is celebrated on 1 October. It was established as a holiday around 1990.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Honduras">Honduras</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Honduras">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Honduras" title="Honduras">Honduras</a>, Children's Day is celebrated on 10 September.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hungary">Hungary</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Hungary">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Children's Week began in Hungary in 1931. Since 1950 it has been reduced to Children's Day, taking place on the last Sunday in May.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haiti">Haiti</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Haiti">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">Haiti</a>, Children's Day is celebrated on 12 June.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hong_Kong">Hong Kong</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Hong Kong">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Children's Day (<a href="/wiki/Traditional_Chinese_characters" title="Traditional Chinese characters">Chinese</a>&#58; <span lang="zh-Hant">兒童節</span>; <a href="/wiki/Jyutping" title="Jyutping">Jyutping</a>&#58; <i><span lang="yue-Latn-jyutping">ji4 tung4 zit3</span></i>) is celebrated on 4 April.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Indonesia">Indonesia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Indonesia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a>, Children's Day is celebrated on 23 July. It was established as a holiday in 1984.<sup id="cite_ref-setgab_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-setgab-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="India">India</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: India">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Bal_Diwas" class="mw-redirect" title="Bal Diwas">Bal Diwas</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Nehru_sweets_oratarians_Nongpoh.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Nehru_sweets_oratarians_Nongpoh.jpg/220px-Nehru_sweets_oratarians_Nongpoh.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="139" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Nehru_sweets_oratarians_Nongpoh.jpg/330px-Nehru_sweets_oratarians_Nongpoh.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d6/Nehru_sweets_oratarians_Nongpoh.jpg/440px-Nehru_sweets_oratarians_Nongpoh.jpg 2x" data-file-width="951" data-file-height="600" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Nehru_sweets_oratarians_Nongpoh.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Nehru distributes sweets among children at <a href="/wiki/Nongpoh" title="Nongpoh">Nongpoh</a>, Meghalaya.</div></div></div>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>, Children's Day is celebrated on 14 November, on the birthday of <a href="/wiki/Jawaharlal_Nehru" title="Jawaharlal Nehru">Jawaharlal Nehru</a>, the first Prime Minister of independent India, who was fondly called <i>Chacha Nehru</i> (Uncle Nehru) or <i>Chachaji</i> (Uncle), and who emphasized the importance of giving love and affection to children, to give him tribute. After his death on 27 May, 1964, it was unanimously decided to celebrate his birthday as <i>Bal Diwas</i> or Children's Day in India.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ireland">Ireland</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Ireland">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Ireland</a>, Universal Children's Day is celebrated on 20 November.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Japan">Japan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Japan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Children%27s_Day_(Japan)" title="Children&#39;s Day (Japan)">Children's Day</a><span style="font-weight: normal">&#32;(<span lang="ja">こどもの日</span><span style="display:none">,</span>&#32;<i>kodomo no hi</i>)</span> is celebrated on 5 May, a <a href="/wiki/Public_holiday" title="Public holiday">National Holiday</a> since 1948, to celebrate the happiness of all children and to express gratitude toward mothers. There is a long tradition, from the 8th century, to celebrate children's day twice a year; 3 March for girls and on 5 May for boys. On 3 March, also known as the <a href="/wiki/Doll_Festival" class="mw-redirect" title="Doll Festival">Doll Festival</a>, Japanese people decorate their households with traditional <a href="/wiki/Heian_Period" class="mw-redirect" title="Heian Period">Heian Period</a> doll sets and <a href="/wiki/Plum" title="Plum">plum</a> blossom, and drink <a href="/wiki/Amazake" title="Amazake">Amazake</a>. On 5 May, also known as 端午の節句 (tango-no sekku), they fly <a href="/wiki/Carp_streamers" class="mw-redirect" title="Carp streamers">carp streamers</a> outside, display <a href="/wiki/Samurai" title="Samurai">Samurai</a> dolls, and eat <a href="/wiki/Chimaki" class="mw-redirect" title="Chimaki">chimaki</a>.
</p><p>There were some who argued in 1948 that 3 March should also be a National Holiday.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Kazakhstan">Kazakhstan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Kazakhstan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The International Children's Day is celebrated annually on 1 June and is established as a national holiday for children. Over 3 million children across Kazakhstan celebrate the holiday with special children's events.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="Lacks source (October 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="North_Korea">North Korea</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: North Korea">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:International_Children%27s_Day_2019.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/International_Children%27s_Day_2019.jpg/220px-International_Children%27s_Day_2019.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="133" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/International_Children%27s_Day_2019.jpg/330px-International_Children%27s_Day_2019.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/International_Children%27s_Day_2019.jpg/440px-International_Children%27s_Day_2019.jpg 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="543" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:International_Children%27s_Day_2019.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>International Children's Day in <a href="/wiki/Taesongsan_Funfair" title="Taesongsan Funfair">Taesongsan Funfair</a>, <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a>, 1 June 2019</div></div></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korean</a> Children's Day is celebrated on 1 June as the International Children's Day (국제 아동절). Before 1945, it was celebrated on 1 May. There is also a day called 조선소년단창립절 (Festival for the establishment of <a href="/wiki/Young_Pioneer_Corps" class="mw-redirect" title="Young Pioneer Corps">Young Pioneer Corps</a>) on 6 June.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="South_Korea">South Korea</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: South Korea">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Children%27s_day_1954.gif" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Children%27s_day_1954.gif/220px-Children%27s_day_1954.gif" decoding="async" width="220" height="144" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Children%27s_day_1954.gif/330px-Children%27s_day_1954.gif 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Children%27s_day_1954.gif/440px-Children%27s_day_1954.gif 2x" data-file-width="750" data-file-height="492" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Children%27s_day_1954.gif" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Children's day in Seoul, <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a>, 5 May 1954</div></div></div>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a>, 5 May is officially recognized as Children's Day (어린이날). Parents often give presents to their children, as well as spend time with them. The children are taken on excursions to zoos, museums, and various venues of children-oriented entertainment.
</p><p>Children's Day was first conceived by innovative Korean students and social leaders on the basis of the <a href="/w/index.php?title=1_March_Movement&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="1 March Movement (page does not exist)">1 March Movement</a> to achieve Korean independence from <a href="/wiki/Korea_under_Japanese_rule" title="Korea under Japanese rule">Japanese colonialism</a>. From <a href="/wiki/Jinju" title="Jinju">Jinju</a>, many people gathered to promote and improve the social status of children and encourage adults to teach awareness of their deprived sovereignty. In 1923,<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> several groups of students studying in Tokyo agreed to designate 1 May as Children's Day. A predominant intellectual figure, <a href="/wiki/Bang_Jeong-hwan" title="Bang Jeong-hwan">Bang Jeong-hwan</a>, greatly contributed to the popularization of the holiday. Because it overlapped with Laborer's Day, Children's Day was moved to 5 May. Bang Jeong-hwan first coined the modern Korean word for children, <i>eorini</i> (어린이), replacing the previous words <i>aenom</i> (애놈) and <i>esaekki</i> (애새끼).<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> Until 1939, Japanese authorities based in Seoul oppressed the movement to stop Korean social activists congregating for the festival. After independence in 1945, the movement to respect children was revived. The children's welfare law written in the constitution officially designated 5 May as Children's Day in 1961. And by 'the law of holiday of government office', Children's day became a holiday in Korea in 1970.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Liberia">Liberia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Liberia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Liberia" title="Liberia">Liberia</a>, Children's day was established as a holiday in 1991.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Laos">Laos</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Laos">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Laos" title="Laos">Laos</a>, Children's Day is celebrated on 1 June.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Maldives">Maldives</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Maldives">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Childrens%27_Day_celebrate_in_Kendhoo,_Maldives.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a6/Childrens%27_Day_celebrate_in_Kendhoo%2C_Maldives.jpg/220px-Childrens%27_Day_celebrate_in_Kendhoo%2C_Maldives.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a6/Childrens%27_Day_celebrate_in_Kendhoo%2C_Maldives.jpg/330px-Childrens%27_Day_celebrate_in_Kendhoo%2C_Maldives.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a6/Childrens%27_Day_celebrate_in_Kendhoo%2C_Maldives.jpg/440px-Childrens%27_Day_celebrate_in_Kendhoo%2C_Maldives.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="480" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Childrens%27_Day_celebrate_in_Kendhoo,_Maldives.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Children's Day celebration in <a href="/wiki/Kendhoo" title="Kendhoo">Kendhoo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Maldives" title="Maldives">Maldives</a></div></div></div>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Maldives" title="Maldives">Maldives</a>, Children's Day (Kudakudhinge Dhuvas) is celebrated on 10 May. On this day all the school children go to school to the event to celebrate Children's Day. The schools that are involved would also organize numerous activities for their pupils.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mauritius">Mauritius</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Mauritius">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Mauritius" title="Mauritius">Mauritius</a>, Children's Day was established in 1991, as the <a href="/wiki/International_Day_of_the_African_Child" title="International Day of the African Child">International Day of the African Child</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Myanmar">Myanmar</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Myanmar">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Myanmar" title="Myanmar">Myanmar</a>, Children's Day is celebrated on 13 February.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mexico">Mexico</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Mexico">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a>, Children's Day ("Día Del Niño") is celebrated 30 April.  On this day teachers in schools organize the day for their children.  In some schools, lessons are suspended for the day.  They organize games, music, and the children bring in their favorite foods to share with others.  Some families also have a day out with their children.  There are special activities for children in parks and sports centers.  Sometimes, also, the children will be given presents by their families.  This is the day when children are honored in Mexico. As it is spring, children wear many bright colors to celebrate their youth and the coming of Spring.
</p><p>Children's Day in Mexico started in 1925. This celebration had its origins during <a href="/wiki/%C3%81lvaro_Obreg%C3%B3n" title="Álvaro Obregón">Álvaro Obregón</a>'s presidential period after the country joined the <a href="/wiki/Geneva_Conventions" title="Geneva Conventions">Geneva Conventions</a> and looking after the wellness of the vulnerable children affected by <a href="/wiki/World_War_I" title="World War I">World War I</a>. Later, the Geneva <a href="/wiki/Declaration_of_the_Rights_of_the_Child" title="Declaration of the Rights of the Child">Declaration of the Rights of the Child</a> was adopted on 26 November 1924 by the League of Nations recognizing that children are the most affected by war events.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> recommended 20 November to celebrate Children's Day throughout the world, but that day coincides with <a href="/wiki/Revolution_Day_(Mexico)" title="Revolution Day (Mexico)">Revolution Day (Mexico)</a>. Also, 30 April was selected in order to avoid 1 May (<a href="/wiki/Labor_Day" title="Labor Day">Labor Day</a>) and the celebrations of <a href="/wiki/Cinco_de_Mayo" title="Cinco de Mayo">Cinco de Mayo</a> (The Day of the Battle of Puebla).
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Malaysia">Malaysia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Malaysia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>It is held traditionally on 1 October. Nowadays it is also celebrated on 20 November (following International Children's Day).
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Moldova">Moldova</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Moldova">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Moldova" title="Moldova">Moldova</a>, International Children's Day is celebrated on 1 June. From 2016, the day has been declared a public holiday.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mongolia">Mongolia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Mongolia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Mongolia" title="Mongolia">Mongolia</a>, the International Children's Day is celebrated on 1 June. It is also known as "Эх үрсийн баяр". In 1 June every kid takes presents, gifts and such more! There are also festivals, sales and sweets!
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mozambique">Mozambique</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Mozambique">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Mozambique" title="Mozambique">Mozambique</a>, the International Children's Day is also celebrated on 1 June .
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Nepal">Nepal</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Nepal">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Nepal" title="Nepal">Nepal</a>, Children's Day (बाल दिवस) is celebrated on Bhadra 29 according to the Nepali Calendar (August–September)after signing the child rights agreement with the UN. Earlier during the Shah Rule, Nepal used to observe Children's day on Bhadra 4 on the birthday of H.M. Queen Mother Ratna Rajya Laxmi Devi Shah. It is celebrated by conducting various programme on various institutions around Nepal. It was established as a holiday in 1990.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="New_Zealand">New Zealand</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=55" title="Edit section: New Zealand">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a>, Children's Day is typically celebrated on the first Sunday in March. It honors children as a <i>taonga</i> (Maori for <i>treasure</i>), and is a day family can relax and share in activities to honor their children. In 2012, the focus was on peace and <i>aroha</i> (<a href="/wiki/M%C4%81ori_language" title="Māori language">Maori</a> for 'love'). New Zealand has high rates of child abuse and family violence. The <a href="/wiki/Government_of_New_Zealand" title="Government of New Zealand">Government of New Zealand</a> has recognized this as one of the most important issues for New Zealanders, with an event such as Children's Day helping to focus on the practice of sharing, loving and caring as well as honoring <i>tamariki</i> (Maori for 'children').<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Nigeria">Nigeria</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: Nigeria">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Children's Day is celebrated on 27 May in <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigeria</a>. It was established as a holiday in 1964. It is a public holiday for Primary and Secondary school children. Due to the large size of the country, only a few groups of children (schools or any other organization) are selected to march past in a parade.
The children are usually given treats such as an outing or doing jobs that adults would normally do. In some situations, primary and secondary school children compete in military parades format for a prize which will be given at the end of the competition.
Religious groups in Nigeria also celebrate children's day in grand style.
Many private and public organizations usually put together children's party for privileged and less privileged children in a bid to give them a sense of belonging. It is also a day media organizations analyze the plight of children in the society and efforts government and nongovernment agencies make to better a lot of children.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Nicaragua">Nicaragua</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Nicaragua">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Nicaragua" title="Nicaragua">Nicaragua</a> the International Children's Day is celebrated on 1 June.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Norway">Norway</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: Norway">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:21._Barnehj%C3%A6lpsdagen_1911_-_no-nb_digifoto_20140819_00111_blds_06915.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/54/21._Barnehj%C3%A6lpsdagen_1911_-_no-nb_digifoto_20140819_00111_blds_06915.jpg/220px-21._Barnehj%C3%A6lpsdagen_1911_-_no-nb_digifoto_20140819_00111_blds_06915.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="139" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/54/21._Barnehj%C3%A6lpsdagen_1911_-_no-nb_digifoto_20140819_00111_blds_06915.jpg/330px-21._Barnehj%C3%A6lpsdagen_1911_-_no-nb_digifoto_20140819_00111_blds_06915.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/54/21._Barnehj%C3%A6lpsdagen_1911_-_no-nb_digifoto_20140819_00111_blds_06915.jpg/440px-21._Barnehj%C3%A6lpsdagen_1911_-_no-nb_digifoto_20140819_00111_blds_06915.jpg 2x" data-file-width="7719" data-file-height="4873" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:21._Barnehj%C3%A6lpsdagen_1911_-_no-nb_digifoto_20140819_00111_blds_06915.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Children's Day in Norway, in 1911</div></div></div>
<p>Children's Day in <a href="/wiki/Norway" title="Norway">Norway</a> is held on 17 May, the same day as <a href="/wiki/Norwegian_Constitution_Day" title="Norwegian Constitution Day">Norwegian Constitution Day</a>, with many children's parades simultaneously celebrating both events and thereby emphasizing the importance of children in Norwegian society.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pakistan">Pakistan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=59" title="Edit section: Pakistan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>, the National Assembly on 16 December 2015 passed a unanimous resolution expressing grief and sadness over the martyrdom of more than 150 students and teachers of Army Public School Peshawar on 16 December 2014. The NA recommended that 16 December should be observed as Pakistan Children Day in memory of the martyrs.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Earlier Children's Day was celebrated on 1 July.In Punjab the Child Rights Cell of Department of Social Welfare Punjab collaborates with UNICEF to celebrate this day. Whereas, The NGO, Voice of Children Islamabad, also celebrates Children's day and arranges activities for children and parents on that day.  The EPO and SFB also celebrate Children's day and arrange fun and interactive sessions for children and parents.
</p><p>For Children's Day, there are many festivals and events organized by schools and organizations, that focus on having fun and lively activities that kids and their families can enjoy. Most charitable organizations also partake in the festivities, by holding functions or partnering with bigger organizations. Thus, everyone joins in to make this day a memorable event each year in Pakistan.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (November 2014)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Palestine">Palestine</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: Palestine">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Children day is celebrated in the <a href="/wiki/State_of_Palestine" title="State of Palestine">State of Palestine</a> on 5 April.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Panama">Panama</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=61" title="Edit section: Panama">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Panama" title="Panama">Panama</a>, Children's Day or Kid's Day was formerly held on 1 November, but was changed by Vivian Fernandez de Torrijos, the wife of President Martin Torrijos (2004–2009), to the third Sunday of July.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Paraguay">Paraguay</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=62" title="Edit section: Paraguay">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Paraguay" title="Paraguay">Paraguay</a>, Children's Day is celebrated on 16 August, day of the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Acosta_%C3%91u" title="Battle of Acosta Ñu">Battle of Acosta Ñu</a>, where it is said that 20,000 men from the Triple Alliance were awaited by a Paraguayan force made up of 3,500 children ages six to fifteen, ordered to hold the Alliance forces while the president Solano Lopez could escape. Even though Paraguay had been already completely defeated, it is said that Lopez forced them to stay and face the enemy, others sources claim that the children volunteered to fight against the Allied forces after their families had been killed by the advancing allied forces (see more in <a href="/wiki/Paraguayan_War" title="Paraguayan War">Paraguayan War</a>). Children's Day is a national holiday, used to remember the event, which happened during the five-year war.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Peru">Peru</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=63" title="Edit section: Peru">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>According to Peruvian law in <a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">Peru</a>, Children's Day (<i>Día del Niño Peruano (Ley Nº 27666) </i>, literally Peruvian Child's Day (Law Nº 27666)) is celebrated every second Sunday of April.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
There is a second celebration every third Sunday of August promoted as the "International Children's Day".
On this day of the year, Peruvian children would typically be congratulated and would receive presents from their parents. Since it is celebrated on Sunday, all special activities in <a href="/wiki/School" title="School">school</a>, such as field trips and the like are done the previous Friday. All major stores offer special discounts on toys, appliances, electronics, clothes, etc.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Philippines">Philippines</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=64" title="Edit section: Philippines">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>, Republic Act No. 10661 declares the month of November as Children's Month in commemoration of the adoption of the Convention on the Rights of the Child by the United Nations General Assembly on 20 November 1989.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Poland">Poland</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=65" title="Edit section: Poland">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:182px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Children%27s_Day,_%C5%81%C3%B3d%C5%BA_Arlekin_Theatre_May_31_01.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Children%27s_Day%2C_%C5%81%C3%B3d%C5%BA_Arlekin_Theatre_May_31_01.jpg/180px-Children%27s_Day%2C_%C5%81%C3%B3d%C5%BA_Arlekin_Theatre_May_31_01.jpg" decoding="async" width="180" height="269" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Children%27s_Day%2C_%C5%81%C3%B3d%C5%BA_Arlekin_Theatre_May_31_01.jpg/270px-Children%27s_Day%2C_%C5%81%C3%B3d%C5%BA_Arlekin_Theatre_May_31_01.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6f/Children%27s_Day%2C_%C5%81%C3%B3d%C5%BA_Arlekin_Theatre_May_31_01.jpg/360px-Children%27s_Day%2C_%C5%81%C3%B3d%C5%BA_Arlekin_Theatre_May_31_01.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2592" data-file-height="3872" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Children%27s_Day,_%C5%81%C3%B3d%C5%BA_Arlekin_Theatre_May_31_01.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Children's Day at Arlekin Theatre, <a href="/wiki/%C5%81%C3%B3d%C5%BA" title="Łódź">Łódź</a>, 2015</div></div></div>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a>, Children's Day (<i>Dzień Dziecka</i>) is celebrated on 1 June. The International Children's Day was introduced in Poland in 1952. It coincides with the beginning of meteorological summer and it is usually treated as a special day, free from lessons, as it takes place near the end of the school year. Schools usually organize special activities for the pupils to celebrate the day, and during the first week of June, is a time of festivities organized in parks and entertainment centers for children.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Portugal_and_some_former_colonies">Portugal and some former colonies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=66" title="Edit section: Portugal and some former colonies">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Portugal" title="Portugal">Portugal</a> (and also at some of its former Asiatic and African colonies such as <a href="/wiki/Guinea-Bissau" title="Guinea-Bissau">Guinea-Bissau</a>, <a href="/wiki/Macau" title="Macau">Macau</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cape_Verde" title="Cape Verde">Cape Verde</a>, <a href="/wiki/East_Timor" title="East Timor">East Timor</a>, <a href="/wiki/Angola" title="Angola">Angola</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mozambique" title="Mozambique">Mozambique</a> and <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Tom%C3%A9_and_Pr%C3%ADncipe" title="São Tomé and Príncipe">São Tomé and Príncipe</a>), Children's Day (Dia da Criança) is celebrated on 1 June.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Romania">Romania</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=67" title="Edit section: Romania">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Romania" title="Romania">Romania</a>, Children's Day (<a href="/wiki/Romanian_language" title="Romanian language">Romanian</a>: "Ziua Copilului") is celebrated on 1 June.  Children often receive presents from parents and other family members. Various events are also organized.
</p><p>On 1 June 2012, International Children's Day was celebrated by the Romanian Government at the Ministry of Labour, Family and Social Protection.<sup id="cite_ref-European_Commission_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-European_Commission-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> Almost 100 children in attendance received a Minister of Children diploma celebrating with parents and grandparents.<sup id="cite_ref-European_Commission_47-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-European_Commission-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>According to the Law 220/2016, starting with 2017, Children's Day is officially a public holiday.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Russia">Russia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Children%27s_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;section=68" title="Edit section: Russia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:RIAN_archive_398877_Festivities_in_Vladivostok_to_celebrate_International_Children%27s_Day.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/RIAN_archive_398877_Festivities_in_Vladivostok_to_celebrate_International_Children%27s_Day.jpg/220px-RIAN_archive_398877_Festivities_in_Vladivostok_to_celebrate_International_Children%27s_Day.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="161" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/RIAN_archive_398877_Festivities_in_Vladivostok_to_celebrate_International_Children%27s_Day.jpg/330px-RIAN_archive_398877_Festivities_in_Vladivostok_to_celebrate_International_Children%27s_Day.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/RIAN_archive_398877_Festivities_in_Vladivostok_to_celebrate_International_Children%27s_Day.jpg/440px-RIAN_archive_398877_Festivities_in_Vladivostok_to_celebrate_International_Children%27s_Day.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="748" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:RIAN_archive_398877_Festivities_in_Vladivostok_to_celebrate_International_Children%27s_Day.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Children of <a href="/wiki/Vladivostok" title="Vladivostok">Vladivostok</a>, <a href="/wiki/Russian_Federation" class="mw-redirect" title="Russian Federation">Russian Federation</a> celebrating the International Children's Day</div></div></div>
